SOURCE DATA FOR THIS SLIDE INSTANCE (verbatim rows from context files):
[Sheet: RichFeatureQueries_Full_2026.xlsx / Full Features] (1 rows)
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-29513 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: APPLICATION PROCESSES | Roadmap Feature: Support four-eye principle in Solon Tax - Approval Workflow | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 392 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As an IRM Admin, I should be able to configure workflows, that enforce four-eyes approval within business processes, ensuring that one user initiates an action and a different user validates and approves it before completion.

*Introduction* 

This feature is a result of PSD-12702 for UBM project, however it is anticipated that all implementations may use this functionality to cover different business cases. As it is described in the related PSD: 

At present, SOLON does not support double attestation (four eye principle) out of the box in human case management, which conflicts with the following requirement specified in SKV's contract (applicable to UBM as well):

 
|​3.2.2.2.1.16|​Functional|​Case Management|​In the software, it shall be possible to configure the actions that require verification (double attestation) by two different case workers during manual handling, including at least:
 - Manual registration of debiting/crediting
 - Manual modification of a transaction on a tax account
 - Manual administration of Swedish and foreign disbursement accounts
 - Manual registration and modification of a disbursement block​|​LKVFM-2.9.306|

 

UBM need the possibility to employ double attestation on human tasks, such that a change affected by the completion of the case is verified by at least 2 distinct case workers. This is for example needed for imposing sanctions on either individual people, credit institutions, or countries, where one case worker would create the case, and another one would validate the right target is being sanctioned, approve the case, turn it back to the initiator, who could then complete the task and thereby enforce the sanction. A rejection should naturally not enforce anything, but require a change in the human task from the initiator, or closing of the case altogether. 

Dependent user stories for sanctions are attached as a PNG. They are not yet created as User Stories in toolkit. Furthermore manual registration of payment methods (e.g. for international bank accounts) require double attestation. It is expected that more functional cases that require double attestation will appear. As such, a generic approach to employing double attestation on a human task flow is needed.

A workaround is being worked on that could support double attestation, but is a process that requires a lot of manual setup (see attachment). If SOLON had the capability of staging a change for entities in a human task (without persisting it), waiting for either approval or rejection, the requirements for double attestation would be a simpler task to support. 

*Functional Requirements*

> An admin must be able to create, edit, and delete workflow templates for different business processes

> An admin must be able to configure the states (e.g., {_}Pending → Submitted → Approved → Completed{_}) and transitions between them. 

> An admin must be able to define one or more approval steps within a workflow. 

> An admin must be able to assign which roles (e.g., Maker, Checker) can perform each workflow step. 

> An admin must be able to enforce that the same user cannot perform both maker and checker roles in the same workflow instance. 

> An admin must be able to define rules for assigning checkers (e.g., based on transaction type, workers profile, business unit, availability).

> An admin must be able to configure whether one or multiple checkers are required before an item moves forward. 

> An admin must be able to set conditions (e.g., value thresholds, registration characteristics) that trigger additional approval steps. 

> An admin must be able to configure escalation paths if approvals are delayed beyond a defined time. 

> An admin must be able to configure which users(roles) receive notifications when an action is required.

> An admin must be able to set reminder frequencies and escalation notifications. 

> An admin must be able to configure who can view pending, approved, or rejected workflow items. 

> An admin must be able to monitor the status of workflow instances (pending, approved, rejected, completed).

> An admin must be able to ensure all workflow actions are logged with user ID, timestamp, and action type. 

> An admin must be able to generate reports on workflow performance (e.g., approval times, bottlenecks, compliance with four-eyes). 

> An admin must be able to define workflow steps once and reuse them across different business processes. 

> An admin must be able to configure workflows without coding, using parameters (roles, thresholds, states). 

> An admin _must be able to maintain multiple versions of a workflow template and activate/deactivate them as needed._

In the revenue-management-batch repository, the following missing jobs marked as BASE, needs to be migrated:

SOURCE DATA FOR THIS SLIDE INSTANCE (verbatim rows from context files):
[Sheet: RichFeatureQueries_Full_2026.xlsx / Full Features] (3 rows)
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-30378 | Roadmap Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Roadmap Initiative: CASE MANAGEMENT | Roadmap Feature: Integration with Luminus (BRA & Audit support)   | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 42 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: To Do | Features Description: * Improve *integration* with Lumenus BRA / Contractual
   Candidate list to generate cases flow (batch)

 * Establish  *integration* with Lumenus Audit Support  (?) / Contractual

Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-12465 | Roadmap Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Roadmap Initiative: CASE MANAGEMENT | Roadmap Feature: Define and Maintain Case Type - Case Worker Profiles - Use Availability - Admin | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 392 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As an admin, I want to use the case worker’s availability as a criterion in a case worker’s profile. So that only case workers that have a certain availability can be assigned to cases for which this case worker’s profile is applicable.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-702 in which requirements have been documented to define what case worker’s profiles are required to perform a certain type of case.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Admin can use the following matching criteria when defining profiles for the most suitable case workers for a specific type of case:
 ** Average Allocation: can be calculated by dividing the sum of the allocated effort of a worker within a given period (from the start date up until the end date of a case) by the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period. Admin can for example define that the average allocation should be equal to or less than 0.8.
 ** Available man-hours: can be calculated by subtracting the sum of the allocated effort of a case worker within a given period (from the start date up until the end date of a case) from the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period. Admin can for example define that a worker should at least have 8 hours unallocated man-hours within a period.
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-12464 | Roadmap Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Roadmap Initiative: CASE MANAGEMENT | Roadmap Feature: Add and Maintain Case - Assign and Unassign Case Workers - Effort - User | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 392 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As a revenue official, I want to assign case workers (user) that have a required profile (e.g. skills, experience and part of a certain organizational unit) to a case while also considering the availability of the suitable candidates, so that a capable worker (user) with sufficient availability can work on and complete the case. Also, I want to see how much effort is involved for each assigned case worker and for the case in total.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-680 in which requirements have been documented to assign and unassign a worker to/from a case. IRM-680 includes a requirement that the user can specify the expected allocation of a case worker for a case.

This feature is related to IRM-12459 in which requirements have been documented to assign and unassign one or more resource calendars to a worker.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Eligible Workers
 ** User can see the average allocation from the case start date up until the case end date for each case worker that meets any of the worker’s profiles for the case. Average allocation can be calculated by dividing the sum of the allocated effort of a case worker from the start date up until the end date of a case by the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period
 ** User can see the availability in man-hours from the case start date up until the case end date for each case worker that meets any of the case worker’s profiles for the case. Available man-hours can be calculated by subtracting the sum of the allocated effort for a case worker from the start date up until the end date of a case from the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period.
 * Worker’s Assignment
 ** User can see what effort has been calculated based on the provided expected allocation for the case worker’s assignment and the resource calendar(s) that are effective for this worker from the case start date up until the case end date. Effort can only be calculated if (1) a start date and end date have been defined for the related case, and (2) an expected allocation has been provided. Period(s) within the start and end date of the case for which no effective resource calendar has been defined for the case worker are considered non-working periods. Assumption is that the effort will be recalculated if (1) the case start or end date are updated, (2) the expected allocation for that case worker for that case is updated, and/or (3) a resource calendar of an assigned case worker that falls within the period in which the case has been scheduled, is updated.
 * User can see the total calculated effort for the case. Total effort is equal to the sum of the effort that was calculated for each case worker that was assigned to the case.

Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-542 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: CIT | Roadmap Feature: CIT - Submit a CIT Return on ICARUS Self Service | Requester: Other | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 14 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Under Analysis | Features Description: As an ICARUS Self Service user, I want to submit a CIT Return form that captures all necessary Information needed to create a tax assessment for CIT.

*Prerequisites*
 An entity should be:
 1. Registered in IRM System, thus have a TIN
 2. Registered for CIT in IRM
 prior to submit a CIT return form.

The following *actions* should be available in ICARUS Self Service: 
 1. Open a CIT Return form, from the list of existing filing obligations.
 2. Create a CIT Return form and save it as a draft. User should be able to open the draft at a later point and proceed with editing.
 3. Print a CIT Return form in a PDF format should be available.
 4. Submit a CIT Return form to the back-end system.

5. Taxpayer should be able to see the submission date ie the date the form was submitted to the revenue authority. 

6. Taxpayer should be able to see a unique form reference number.

 

The following *validations* on the CIT Return form should be available in ICARUS Self Service. Note that these are only sample validation rules since these may differentiate per country:
 # In Section "Filing Period Details" Fields "Filing Period Start and End Dates" create a validation for filing period based on the filing frequency defined to verify the period selected is complaint. Ex. If filing frequency is annual then 12 month period should be selected.
 # In Section "Filing Period Details" Field "If you do not have to complete ... please tick this box" create a validation when this field is selected then remaining input amount sections to calculate CIT should not be available to edit. Tax amount for this period should be set to zero. 
 # In Section "Net Income" only fields "Returns and Allowances, Cost of Goods Sold, Depreciation and Amortization" should be allowed to accept negative values (Zero value should be allowed). 
 # In Section "Final Tax Assessment"when field "Other Adjustments" has a value different than zero then Attachment Category "Miscellaneous related attachments" should be required prior submitting the form.

SOURCE DATA FOR THIS SLIDE INSTANCE (verbatim rows from context files):

Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-790 | Roadmap Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Roadmap Initiative: CONTACT MANAGEMENT | Roadmap Feature: Send Outbound Message Automatically to Multiple Recipients - Admin | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 358.4 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As an admin, I want to automatically send a copy of a specific outbound message (e.g. letter, email or text message) to different types of recipients (e.g. taxpayer and tax agent), so that the information in the outbound message can be exchanged with all relevant parties.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-786 and IRM-789 where requirements have been documented to send an outbound letter and outbound email / text messages automatically to a single party.

*Functional Requirements*

Admin can enter literal values and/or reference values that will be known at run-time for input parameters that admin has defined for this type of contact and that can be used to automatically select the type of recipients that need to be considered for this type of outbound message, and automatically select a recipient for each type of recipient (based on rules defined by admin). These values can be defined on a 'establish and/or record contact' task within a specific type of business process (see IRM-785).

When executing the 'establish and/or record contact' task on an instance of this type of business process, the system will automatically generate all outbound messages, store these messages, finalize the messages, select a communication channel for each recipient and send the finalized outbound messages via the selected communication channels (e.g. print letter or send email).
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-775 | Roadmap Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Roadmap Initiative: CONTACT MANAGEMENT | Roadmap Feature: Define and Maintain Contact Types - Select Recipients - Admin | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 392 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As an admin, I want to define and maintain rules to determine what recipient(s) need to receive a copy of a certain type of outbound message (e.g. certain type of letter, email or SMS), so that duplicate messages can be send to all parties that need to be informed.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-772 in which requirements have been documented to define and maintain different types of contacts.

Recipients will receive the same information or almost the same information. For example, one letter could contain text to explain that this letter is a copy of the letter that has been sent to the taxpayer representative.
Relevant to https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-774 

*Functional Requirements*
 * Admin can define rules to determine what types of recipients must receive a copy of a specific type of outbound message under certain circumstances. For example, if a certain type of letter is sent to the recipient type 'taxpayer' then a copy of this letter may have to be sent to the recipient type 'tax agent' and/or recipient type 'spouse'.
 * Admin can define rules to determine the recipient for each type of recipient that will receive a copy of the message. For example, find the 'tax agent' that is representing a 'taxpayer' for a specific type of tax. Input parameters defined on the contact type can be used to select the recipients. Values for these input parameters can be provided at design time (literal values) or can be provided at run-time.
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-774 | Roadmap Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Roadmap Initiative: CONTACT MANAGEMENT | Roadmap Feature: Define and Maintain Different Types of Recipients - Admin | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 130.9 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As an admin, I want to define and maintain different types of recipients for outbound messages, so that it can be indicated to what type of recipients a specific message (e.g. letter or email) must be send.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Admin can define a new type of recipient. Examples of properties of a recipient are a code and a description.
 * Admin can search a type of recipient
 * Admin can update a type of recipient
 * Admin can delete a type of recipient provided there are no referential constraints

 ** User will select one channel. 
 * *Generation and results*
 ** User can generate the outbound messages/emails for the recipients selected.
 ** Different types of recipients may receive different outbound message content. (Based on [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-774] ) Admin need to define the contact template per recipient.  
Examples: 
One outbound message could contain text to explain that this outbound message is a copy of the outbound message that has been sent to another type of recipient.
Address requested in contact template as well as balance is adjusted as per party selected. 
Generation requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients. (to be moved to a new feature).
 ** User can regenerate the outbound messages. Regeneration requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can finalize the generated outbound messages.
 ** User can send the finalized outbound messages via the selected communication channel. Send requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can store the outbound messages. Storage requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can see the results of the emailing/sms if integration allows so (as per  IRM-27816 ) 
 ** Solution should be applicable to [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-28177]

 ** Errors/exceptions appears if one of the recipients have incorrect/missing contact details for the selected channel and none of the batch  is sent. 
"Mass contact generation failed" 
"Mass contact send failed"

SOURCE DATA FOR THIS SLIDE INSTANCE (verbatim rows from context files):
[Sheet: RichFeatureQueries_Full_2026.xlsx / Full Features] (1 rows)
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-28521 | Roadmap Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Roadmap Initiative: DOCUMENT MANAGEMENT INTEGRATION | Roadmap Feature: Generic component - Support for Embedded 3rd-Party Digital Signature and Document Preview Components in RM pages | Requester: Other | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 11.2 | Feature Priority: p1 | Feature Status: Closed | Features Description: As an delivery team and admin I need the ability to integrate 3rd-party components such as digital signature dialogs and embedded document/PDF previewers into the Solon UI, so that we can support customer-specific implementations.
As a revenue authority user, I want to preview forms and assist taxpayers in digitally signing documents directly within the Registration Module (RM), in order to comply with national requirements and improve support service at physical desks.

On these Solon will not provide any out of the self integration with these tools but will provide a widget to enable partners on that. 

*Introduction*

According to the Lithuanian law, when signing documents electronically, the user should be able to preview the document in the Web page. Furthermore, the customers want to be able to preview signed or unsigned documents within the web app.
Moreover, there are user flows provided by the client, where users need to preview PDF documents directly within the application. However, the current UI/JSON schema system does not support rendering or embedding PDF viewers, making it impossible to include this functionality through the schema.

Currently, Solon's UI metadata schema (UI/JSON) does not support rendering embedded components like PDF viewers or signature popups. As a result, these features cannot be implemented declaratively through configuration alone. Similar components will be used in ISS by LT delivery teams  (using external portal platform). 
Relevant: 
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/PSD-11428]
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/PSD-12028] 

Solon {*}will not deliver native integrations with specific 3rd-party signature providers or preview tools{*}. However, to support flexibility and enable integration at project level, Solon will provide a generic UI extension mechanism (widget) that can be configured to load and render such external components.

+Considerations+ 
 * _This widget/tag will allow embedding or linking to external components,  such as:_
 ** _PDF  document viewers (e.g. in form page preview form and attachments in a relevant preview mode)_
 *** _External digital signature modules._
_WHAT IS/could be  INCLUDED IN THE iframe and the support of all its usages is Out of scope_ 
_In scope: Be able to add iframes in modals and pages._ 
 ** _The new tag if used in an appropriate widget that is expected to be implemented by delivery , it will be able to support_ 
 *** _rendering the embedded content inline_ 
 *** _or  opening it as a dialog/popup/modal. (such as receiving input request from digital signature app)_
 *** _being triggerable by actions of user (e.g. sign button)_
 *** _pass parameters  via urls or post messages_ 
 *** _return control to Solon tax ui on success of the process (e.g. sign properly) ._ 

 

*Functional requirements*
 * A new *custom widget framework  (i.e.*  *widget-based framework* *using* *secure iframe embedding)* will be introduced in the UI schema system.
 ** Product based on type of widget  (pdf viewer, digital signature)  the proper sandbox attributes should be used
(iframes preferably should have the {{sandbox}} attribute to restrict the content of the embedded page. Any features that are needed (execute scripts, submit forms, etc.) can be explicitly enabled per case when needed).
 ** Closing window callbacks may be functional. 
 ** Be agnostic to signature providers.
 ** Be reusable / configurable 

Out of scope : 
Ui interaction/ post messages 
Custom error messages 

 

*Assumption* :
Integration is {*}properly implemented{*}.
The delivery teams must ensure that the embedded solutions conform to {*}data protection{*}, {*}security policies{*}, and *access control rules* already applied in Solon.

 

*Documentation*

Document all the above adjustments and any suggestion on good usage of the iframe while posting messages. 

 

*Non functional requirements*

Performance and Security DODs should be fulfilled.

Flow :

*E-Signature Workflow Overview*
 # *User Initiates Signing* (frontend)

The user clicks the *"Sign"* button.
 # *Signing Initialization Request* (backend)

A request is sent to the {*}electronic signature service{*}, which:
 * Uploads the files to the {*}signature provider{*}.
 * Initializes the signing process with a specified returnUrl, used to redirect the user back to our system after signing.
 * Returns an {*}external signing UID{*}.

 # *Popup with Embedded Signing UI* (frontend)

A popup window is opened containing an iframe.
The iframe loads the signing page using the URL that includes the *external signing UID* as a query parameter.

*_[DASKALAKIS Ioannis] Please provide, if possible, some more details on the authentication and authorization scheme that may need to be followed to facilitate loading service’s provider URL for the given UID with  the User’s  browser session._*

*_No authentication needs to be done from the browser. Only the backend IP needs to be whitelisted on the service provider and our service accepting the callback needs to be exposed and reachable by the service provider. We have started a discussion about this on another channel, still waiting for a response._*
 # *User Signs Documents* (frontend)

The user completes the signing process within the loaded iframe page.
 # *Callback and Document Handling* (backend)

Our service receives a *callback* from the signature provider when the document status changes (e.g., signing completed).
At this point, we:
 * {*}Download{*}the signed version of the document from the provider.
 * {*}Validate{*}the signed document.
 * {*}Upload{*}it via the document-management

*_[DASKALAKIS Ioannis] This, along with #3, suggests that any document exchange between our system and the signature provider will only take place via service API calls with an adapter implemented in the scope of the project. Please confirm._*

*_Yes, that is correct._*
 # *User Redirection and UI Update* (frontend)

After signing, the user sees a *success message* on the provider's page and is *redirected to the* {*}returnUrl{*}.
If we are able to detect this redirect within the popup, we can:
 * Automatically {*}close the popup{*}.
 * {*}Load the signed document{*}and its metadata in our system for the user to review.

*_[DASKALAKIS Ioannis] Is this required to be a document preview functionality, or it is a direct document download?_*

SOURCE DATA FOR THIS SLIDE INSTANCE (verbatim rows from context files):

Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-16272 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: PIT | Roadmap Feature: PIT - File Original Personal Income Tax Return from Self Service – User | Requester: Other | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 14 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Under Analysis | Features Description: As a self service user, I want to file an original personal income tax return for a specific filing period, so that I can meet my obligation to file a personal income tax return with correct data and on time as stipulated in the tax law.

*Introduction*

Personal income tax return that will be presented on the self service will have the same form sections and form fields as the example personal income tax return that has been described in IRM-14601.

Assumption is that the following self service requirements related to personal income tax are already supported:
 * User can login to the self service portal to deal with the tax matters for a specific party in a specific to which this user has been granted access
 * User can see what filing obligations exist for this party in a specific role for personal income tax and see the status of each of these obligations
 * User can see the personal income tax assessment for a specific filing / payment obligation
 * User can see what payment obligations exist for personal income tax assessments for which this specific party in a specific role is liable
 * User can see what payment obligations exist for any additional charges that have been levied towards a personal tax assessment (e.g. late payment interest) and for which this party in a specific role is considered liable
 * User can pay a liability that exists for a personal income tax assessment and any related charges for this party in a specific role
 * User can see the balance for personal income tax for this party in a specific role

Following self service requirements related to the personal income tax have not been implemented yet and are not in scope of this feature.
 * User can see that income that was paid by employers to this party in a specific role, and that the taxes and social contributions that were already deducted by these employers, are prefilled in the income form section of a pending personal income tax return
 * User can save a draft of a pending personal income tax return, and can open and complete a draft personal income tax return at a later point in time
 * User can see a notification that the personal income tax has been assessed for the filing period for which the personal income tax return was submitted

*Functional Requirements*
 * User can create a pending original personal income tax return for a filing period for which no original personal income tax has been submitted yet. User can see the form sections for taxpayer details, bank account details, income details, details on deductions, cost of living details, final tax assessment and attachments, and the related form fields as described in IRM-14601. Any meta data related to a personal income tax return (e.g. form source, related risk observations and related bill segments) should not be shown on the self service.
 * User can see that the taxpayer details and bank account details are prefilled in a pending personal income tax return
 * User can fill in the necessary details in the bank account details, income details, details on deductions, cost of living details, final tax assessment and attachments form sections
 * User can submit the personal income tax return once completed
 * User can see if there are any validation exceptions that prevent the pending personal income tax return from being submitted. User can navigate from a validation exception to the related form section and form field(s) to resolve any issues.
 * User can open a submitted personal income tax return to see what data was included in that return
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-16273 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: PIT | Roadmap Feature: PIT - Amend Original Personal Income Tax Return from Self Service – User | Requester: Other | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 14 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Under Analysis | Features Description: As a self service user, I want to amend an already submitted original personal income tax return, so that changes in my income or deductions are reflected in the adjusted personal income tax return.

*Introduction*

This feature is related to IRM-16272 in which requirements have been documented to enable a self service user to file an original personal income tax return for a specific filing period.

Amended personal income tax return that will be presented on the self service will have the same form sections and form fields as the example personal income tax return that has been described in IRM-14601.

This feature is related to IRM-1973 in which requirements have been documented to record adjustments to the data in an input form that was already posted and post any differences that result from these adjustments.

*Functional Requirements*
 * User can amend an original personal income tax return that was submitted and processed. User can only amend the personal income tax return for the current filing period or for the two prior filing periods. And a user can amend an original personal income tax return more than once. User cannot amend an original personal income tax return if the original personal income tax return has not been submitted or processed yet. If an original income tax return was already amended, then the user can only amend the income tax return again if the previously amended return has also been submitted and processed.
 * User can see that the pending amended personal income tax return is prefilled with data from the submitted and processed original personal income tax return or from the latest submitted and processed personal income tax return that amended this original personal income tax return.
 * User can update the necessary details in the bank account details, income details, details on deductions, cost of living details, final tax assessment and attachments form sections of the pending amended personal income tax return
 * User can submit the pending amended personal income tax return once completed
 * User can see if there are any validation exceptions that prevent the pending amended personal income tax return from being submitted. User can navigate from a validation exception to the related form section and form field(s) to resolve any issues.
 * User can see what amendments have been submitted when for a specific original personal income tax return
 * User can open a submitted amended personal income tax return to see what data was included in that return
 * Any updates to the personal income tax return input form, form rules and process that have been implemented in the Revenue Management application (see IRM-14601), that are required to support amended tax returns are also in scope of this feature. When processing an amended original personal income tax return in the Revenue Management application, the difference between the personal income tax assessment in this return and the assessment of the original personal income tax return or the latest submitted and processed personal income tax return that amended this original personal income tax return should be posted.
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-19256 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: PIT | Roadmap Feature: PIT -  Support saving a declaration form in ISS where calculated tax is displayed prior submitting  | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 7.699999999999999 | Feature Priority: p1 | Feature Status: Ready for Dev | Features Description: As a taxpayer I want to be able to see calculated tax in a declaration form (ie VAT) in taxpayers' portal prior submitting and save this as a draft form, so as to be able to meet requirements for Greek demo.

*Functional Requirement*

> User can see in  ISS a tax declaration form ie VAT total tax amount calculated prior submitting the form, save form as a draft and then open to submit.

This feature is related to IRM-3447 in which requirements have been doccumented to see an overview of a taxpayer account on the self service.

Some example wireframes have been attached to this feature.  In case the content on the wireframes differs from the functional requirements, then the functional requirement should be used as input when implementing this feature.

 * User can see registration details of the taxpayer.

Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-5111 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: SELF SERVICE FILING & PAYMENTS | Roadmap Feature: SS Payments - See Filing Obligation Details - Part 2 | Requester: Other | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 392 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: To Do | Features Description: As a self service user, I want to see the details of a specific filing obligation for a specific taxpayer, so that I can see what forms have been created and/or already filed as a result of this obligation, what amounts have been assessed as a result of filing these forms, and what other information has been exchanged with the revenue authority related to this filing obligation such as supporting documents and notices.

*Introduction*

Some example wireframes have been attached to this feature. In case the content on the wireframes differs from the functional requirements, then the functional requirement should be used as input when implementing this feature.

*Functional Requirements*
 * User can see the details of a specific filing obligation for a specific taxpayer

 ** Actions:

 *** {color:#172b4d}User can open a new or draft amended tax return form for a filing obligation. Assumption is that the correct tax return form is opened for the specific tax type for which the overview is provided. Also, the assumption is that the tax return form can be prefilled with data that is already known - for example the taxpayer details, filing period details and data from the original tax return. User can only open a new or draft amended tax return if an original tax return has been submitted for this filing obligation. Assumption is that the user can only amend a tax return for specific tax types (e.g. for corporate income tax).{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}User can open a payment form (see IRM-3542 for an example of a payment form) to pay the sum of all current positive balances of any payment obligations that are related to a specific filing obligation (e.g. late filing penalty or tax assessment and any related charges that were added after filing a tax return for this filing obligation). Assumption is that the payment form can be prefilled with data that is already known - for example the taxpayer details and the payment obligation details. User can only open a payment form if there is an outstanding amount that needs to be paid for these payment obligations.{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}User can open a form to request a refund if an overpayment exists for one or more payment obligations that are related to a specific filing obligation (e.g. late filing penalty or tax assessment and any related charges that were added after filing a tax return for this filing obligation). Assumption is that the refund request form can be prefilled with data that is already known - for example the taxpayer details and the details of the payment obligations for which an overpayment exists. User can only open a refund request form if an overpayment amount exists for any of the payment obligations.{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}User can open a form to request to offset an overpayment that exists for one or more payment obligations that are related to a specific filing obligation (e.g. late filing penalty or tax assessment and any related charges that were added after filing a tax return for this filing obligation). Assumption is that the request overpayment offset form can be prefilled with data that is already known - for example the taxpayer details and the overpayment amount that can be offset.{color}

 *** {color:#c1c7d0}User can upload a supporting document that can be used by the revenue authority to validate the content of the submitted tax return. User can only upload a document if the obligation to file a tax return has been met.
 *** User can open a financial overview (see IRM-3452) for the payment obligations that are related to a specific filing obligation (e.g. late filing penalty or tax assessment and any related charges that were added after filing a tax return for this filing obligation).
 * User can see what amounts have been assessed related to a specific filing obligation (e.g. late filing penalty or tax assessment that was added after filing a tax return for this filing obligation). Any charges (e.g. late payment penalty or interest) that are levied towards these original assessments are not considered in this overview.
 ** Data set - can contain data for multiple assessments
 *** Filing type: the type of submission that was done (e.g. submit preliminary, original or amended tax return)
 *** Letter reference number: unique reference number of the assessment notice in which the taxpayer was informed about the assessment
 *** Assessed amount: the amount that was assessed{color}

 
 * {color:#172b4d}User can see what draft tax returns exist for a specific filing obligation. These tax returns have not been submitted yet.{color}
 ** {color:#172b4d}Data set - can contain data for multiple draft tax returns - most often just one draft form{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Form type: the type of form that was saved as a draft{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Form reference number: the reference number of the form that was saved as a draft{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Last updated date: the date the draft form was last updated{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Status: the status of the form that was saved as a draft (e.g. saved){color}
 ** {color:#172b4d}Actions:{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}User can open the draft tax return (see IRM-3539 for an example of a value added tax return form){color}
 * {color:#172b4d}User can see what supporting documents have been uploaded for a specific filing obligation.{color}
 ** {color:#172b4d}Data set - can contain data for multiple supporting documents{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Document type: the type of supporting document that was submitted to the revenue authority{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Document reference number: a unique reference number of the supporting document that was submitted to the revenue authority{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Submission date: the date the supporting document was submitted to the revenue authority{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Status: the status of submitting a supporting document (e.g. submitted){color}
 ** {color:#172b4d}Actions:{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}User can open a supporting document{color}
 * {color:#172b4d}User can see what letters (e.g. reminder letter, notice letter) were sent to the taxpayer by the revenue authority.{color}
 ** {color:#172b4d}Data set:{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Letter type: the type of letter that was sent to the taxpayer{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Letter reference number: a unique reference for the letter that was sent to the taxpayer{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Description: a description of the letter that was sent to the taxpayer{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}Letter date: the date the letter was considered to have been delivered to the taxpayer{color}
 ** {color:#172b4d}Actions:{color}
 *** {color:#172b4d}User can open a letter (see attached wireframe){color}

Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-3545 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: SELF SERVICE FILING & PAYMENTS | Roadmap Feature: SS Payments - See Payment Details | Requester: Other | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 392 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As a self service user, I want to see the details of a specific payment, so that I can understand when and how the payment was made, understand what was paid and see the related payment receipt.

*Introduction*

Some example wireframes have been attached to this feature. In case the content on the wireframes differs from the functional requirements, then the functional requirement should be used as input when implementing this feature.

*Functional Requirements*
 * User can see the details of a specific payment
 ** Data set:
 *** Payment date: the date on which a payment was made by the user
 *** Payment method: the method that was used to make the payment
 *** Amount paid: the amount that was paid by the user
 *** Status: the status of the payment that was made by the user (e.g. accepted and cancelled)
 * User can see what payment form was submitted to make the payment
 * Data set
 ** Form type: the type of form that was submitted
 ** Form reference number: the reference number of the form that was submitted
 ** Submission date: the date the form was submitted
 ** Status: the status of the form that was submitted (e.g. submitted, being processed or processed)
 * Actions:
 ** User can open a submitted payment form (see IRM-3542 for an example of a payment form)


 * User can see the payment receipt that was provided after having completed the payment
 ** Data set:
 *** Receipt number: a unique reference for the payment receipt that was provided
 *** Creation date: the date the receipt was created
 ** Actions:
 *** User can open the receipt (see attached wireframe)
 * User can see what was paid with the payment.
 ** Data set:
 *** Tax type: description of the tax type to which the payment was distributed for the taxpayer
 *** Period: description of the period (if any) to which the payment was distributed for the taxpayer
 *** Amount paid: the amount that was paid to the specific tax type and period for the taxpayer

*Introduction*

Some example wireframes have been attached to this feature. In case the content on the wireframes differs from the functional requirements, then the functional requirement should be used as input when implementing this feature.

*Functional Requirements*
 * User can see the payments that were made for a specific taxpayer
 ** Filters:
 *** Year: user can choose to view the payments for all years or for a specific year
 *** Status: user can choose to view the payments with any status or to view only payments with a specific status
 ** Data set:
 *** Payment date: the date on which a payment was made by the user
 *** Payment method: the method that was used to make the payment
 *** Amount paid: the amount that was paid by the user
 *** Status: the status of the payment that was made by the user (e.g. accepted, rejected and cancelled)
 ** Actions:
 *** User can open the details of a specific payment (see IRM-3545)
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-3542 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: SELF SERVICE FILING & PAYMENTS | Roadmap Feature: SS  Payments - Submit Payment Form | Requester: Other | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 392 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As a self service user, I want fill in and submit a payment form to pay the amounts owed for certain payment obligations, so that I can meet these payment obligations towards the revenue authority.

*Introduction*

Some example wireframes have been attached to this feature. In case the content on the wireframes differs from the functional requirements, then the functional requirement should be used as input when implementing this feature.

*Functional Requirements*
 * User can see a payment form
 ** Data set:
 *** Taxpayer details
 **** Taxpayer name: name of the taxpayer for which the payment obligations exist - assumption is that the taxpayer name can be prefilled and is read-only
 **** Identification type: the primary identification type of the taxpayer - assumption is that the identification type can be prefilled and is read-only
 **** Identification number: the primary identification number of the taxpayer - assumption is that the identification type can be prefilled and is read-only
 *** Payment details
 **** Payment method: payment methods that the user can select from - payment method credit card is used as an example in this example
 **** Payment service provider: payment service providers that the user can select from - payment service provider can only be selected if there are multiple payment service providers that support the selected payment method
 **** Credit card: types of credit cards that the user can choose from
 **** Credit card number: number on the user's credit card
 **** Expiry date month: credit card will expire at the end of this month
 **** Expiry date year: credit card will expire in this year
 **** CVV Security Code: security code that can be found on the back of the credit card
 **** Name: name that is displayed on the front of the card
 *** Payment Obligations - can contain data of multiple payment obligations
 **** Tax type: description of the tax type for which the payment obligation exists - assumption is that this information is prefilled based on the payment obligations that were selected on a previous page (see for example IRM-3451 and IRM-3541) and read-only
 **** Period: description of the period (if any) for which the obligation to pay certain liabilities exist (e.g. late filing penalty or tax assessment and any related charges that were added after filing a tax return for this period) - assumption is that this information is prefilled based on the payment obligations that were selected on a previous page (see for example IRM-3451 and IRM-3541) and read-only
 **** Payable amount: the total outstanding amount for a payment obligation - assumption is that this information is prefilled based on the payment obligations that were selected on a previous page (see for example IRM-3451 and IRM-3541) and read-only
 **** Payment amount: amount that the user can enter to indicate how much should be paid for a specific payment obligation - assumption is that the payment amount is equal to the payable amount by default
 **** Total payable amount: the sum of the payable amounts of the selected payment obligations - assumption is that this amount is calculated and read-only
 **** Total payment amount: the sum of the amount that will be paid for the selected payment obligations - assumption is that this amount is calculated and read-only
 ** Actions:
 *** User can print a payment form as a PDF
 *** User can submit a payment form once the form has been filled in. User can see if there are any validation issues that need to be resolved before the value added tax return can be submitted. User can see a confirmation if the payment was successfully processed (see attached wireframe). User can open a payment receipt if the payment was successfully processed (see attached wireframe).
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-3541 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: SELF SERVICE FILING & PAYMENTS | Roadmap Feature: SS  Payments - See Current Payment Obligations | Requester: Other | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 392 | Feature Priority: p3 | Feature Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Features Description: As a self service user, I want to see what payment obligations exist for a specific taxpayer, so that I can take action to pay what is owed by the taxpayer to the revenue authority.

*Introduction*

Some example wireframes have been attached to this feature. In case the content on the wireframes differs from the functional requirements, then the functional requirement should be used as input when implementing this feature.

*Functional Requirements*
 * User can see the current payment obligations for a specific taxpayer
 ** Data set:
 *** Tax type: description of the tax type for which the obligation to pay certain liabilities exist
 *** Period: description of the period (if any) for which the obligation to pay certain liabilities exist (e.g. late filing penalty or tax assessment and any related charges that were added after filing a tax return for this period)
 *** Payable amount: the amount that the taxpayer is obliged to pay for the specific tax type in the specific period (if any)
 *** Status: the status of the payment action that the taxpayer is obliged to perform - user can see whether the action is considered overdue or not
 ** Actions:
 *** User can select one or more payment obligations for which the user wants to take action to pay what is owed to the revenue authority
 *** User can open a payment form (see IRM-3542) to provide the information that is required to pay the selected payment obligations
Issue Type: Feature | IRM: IRM-374 | Roadmap Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Roadmap Initiative: SELF SERVICE FILING & PAYMENTS | Roadmap Feature: SS Payments - Initiate Payment from Self Service Portal - User | Requester: GRC | PI: PI29 | Estimate: 507.5 | Feature Priority: p2 | Feature Status: Under Analysis | Features Description: As a taxpayer, I want to see and pay my outstanding liabilities from the self service portal, so that I can understand and meet my payment obligations towards the revenue authority.

*Introduction*

This feature describes how the taxpayer can use the taxpayer self service portal to initiate a payment to pay outstanding liabilities.

The steps the taxpayer must follow to initiate and complete a payment may vary depending on the type of integration between ICARUS and the payment service providers (a.k.a. payment gateways or PSPs). Integration types to consider are (1) hosted - taxpayer leaves self service portal to complete payment on PSP portal, (2) direct post - PSP page that is used to complete the payment is embedded in a frame on self service portal and (3) non-hosted - self service portal provides features to capture all payment details and uses an API to submit details to the PSP. This feature describes the requirements assuming the 3rd type of integration is used.

Revenue authorities can depending on the requirements provide various options on the self service portal to pay outstanding liabilities, including for example (1) pay party role, (2) pay specific tax account, (3) pay a specific filing period, (4) pay a specific pay plan, (5) pay a specific collection notice, (6) pay a specific tax return, or (7) pay a specific single assessed liability (e.g. tax, penalty or interest). This feature describes the requirements for the 3rd and 7th option.

Revenue authorities can depending on the requirements provide various payment methods on the self service portal to pay outstanding liabilities. Examples include (1) credit card, (2) debit card, (3) PayPal and other similar services, (4) M-Pesa, Paym and other similar services, (5) direct debit, (6) PDS2 and other similar services and (7) guarantees registered at the revenue authority. This feature describes the requirements for the 1st option.

Revenue authorities and/or payment service providers may charge convenience fees. Information on any applicable fees must be presented to the portal user before submitting the payment. Convenience fee requirements will be documented in another feature.

As credit card details are used in the self service portal, the product should cater for features to allow the revenue authority to be PCI-DSS compliant. Relevant PCI-DSS requirements will be documented in another feature.

*Functional requirements*
 * User can select outstanding liabilities for payment. Examples in scope for this feature are:
 ** User can see a list with outstanding liabilities. Examples of properties to display in the list are the debt category, revenue type, filing period, notice reference number, payable amount and status of the liability (e.g. pending or overdue). User can select one or more outstanding liabilities for payment. See example on attached screenshot 'ICARUS Self Service Pay Specific Assessed Liabilities Example.png'. Multi-select and passing data to another action will be implemented as part of IRM-401.
 ** User can see the assessed liabilities (including outstanding liabilities) for a specific filing period (on the filing obligation details page). User can choose to pay all outstanding liabilities for the filing period or choose to pay a single assessed liability. See example on attached screenshot 'ICARUS Self Service Pay Specific Filing Period Example.png'.
 * User can enter the following data in the sample payment form.
 See example of form in attached screenshot 'ICARUS Self Service Payment Form Credit Card Example.png'
 ** Taxpayer Details
 *** Taxpayer Name (prefilled and read-only)
 *** Identification Type (prefilled and read-only)
 *** Identification Number (prefilled and read-only)
 ** Payment Details
 *** Payment Method (configurable list)
 *** Payment Service Provider (configurable list)
 Payment Service Provider field is only shown if there are multiple Payment Service Providers defined that support the selected Payment Method
 *** Credit Card (configurable list)
 *** Credit Card Number
 *** Expiry Date - Month
 *** Expiry Date - Year
 *** CVV Security Code
 *** Name on Card
 ** Payment Obligations (multiple; prefilled based on selected outstanding liabilities)
 *** Debt Category (prefilled)
 *** Revenue Type (prefilled)
 *** Period (prefilled)
 *** Reference Number (prefilled)
 *** Payable Amount (prefilled)
 *** Payment Amount
 User can enter the payment amount for each row with outstanding liability details.
 *** Total Payable Amount (calculated)
 *** Total Payment Amount (calculated)
 * User can see currency symbol for amounts.
 * User can save a draft of the payment form.
 * User can print the payment form to PDF.
 * User can submit the payment form to the Payment Service Provider.
 * User can see a payment confirmation message if the payment was successfully processed after submission. Examples of data displayed on the payment confirmation are the payment status, payment date, payment amount and payment receipt number. See example on attached screenshot 'ICARUS Self Service Payment Confirmation.png'.
 * If the payment could not be processed after submission, the user can see the validation exceptions in the payment form. Examples of reasons why the payment could not be processed are invalid credit card number and credit card is expired. The user should be able to correct the data entered in the payment form or to abort the attempt to pay
 * User can open the payment receipt. Examples of data displayed on the payment receipt are taxpayer name, taxpayer identification type, taxpayer identification number, taxpayer address, payment method, payment date, payment amount, and information about what was paid (e.g. tax type and filing period) (will be handled by IRM-380)
 * User can print the payment receipt to PDF (will be handled by IRM-380)

 *Note* that the form described above refers to the case of paying transactions. A different form should be created for the case of paying an obligation (Pay button on upper part of "ICARUS Self Service Pay Specific Filing Period Example.png"
